Once the folder is selected, the path is displayed in the EXE path text field.\r\n\r\nSelect an option from the Options drop down. If no option is selected none is supplied on the command line. These parameters are described in the PDFToText.exe documentation.\r\n\r\nClick on the ‚ÄòSave to Clipboard‚Äô button to copy the command line to the clipboard.\r\n\r\nFrom the ‚ÄòWindows System‚Äô folder displayed with the Start menu, select the ‚ÄòCommand Prompt‚Äô program to open the console. Users get to experiment with various options without having to copy and paste various file paths or other settings piecemeal.
